declare @project_admin int
select @project_admin = count(1)
	from sessions
	inner join project_user_xref on pu_user = se_user
	and pu_admin = 1
	where se_id = '16088cb5-2541-4c37-9f16-89c13bbfe945';

select us_id, us_admin,
us_username, us_firstname, us_lastname,
isnull(us_email,'') us_email,
isnull(us_bugs_per_page,10) us_bugs_per_page,
isnull(us_forced_project,0) us_forced_project,
us_use_fckeditor,
us_enable_bug_list_popups,
og.*,
isnull(us_forced_project, 0 ) us_forced_project,
isnull(pu_permission_level, 2) pu_permission_level,
@project_admin [project_admin]
from sessions
inner join users on se_user = us_id
inner join orgs og on us_org = og_id
left outer join project_user_xref
	on pu_project = us_forced_project
	and pu_user = us_id
where se_id = '16088cb5-2541-4c37-9f16-89c13bbfe945'
and us_active = 1

/* get_bug_posts */
select
a.bp_bug,
a.bp_comment,
isnull(us_username,'') [us_username],
case rtrim(us_firstname)
	when null then isnull(us_lastname, '')
	when '' then isnull(us_lastname, '')
	else isnull(us_lastname + ', ' + us_firstname,'')
	end [us_fullname],
isnull(us_email,'') [us_email],
a.bp_date,
datediff(s,a.bp_date,getdate()) [seconds_ago],
a.bp_id,
a.bp_type,
isnull(a.bp_email_from,'') bp_email_from,
isnull(a.bp_email_to,'') bp_email_to,
isnull(a.bp_email_cc,'') bp_email_cc,
isnull(a.bp_file,'') bp_file,
isnull(a.bp_size,0) bp_size,
isnull(a.bp_content_type,'') bp_content_type,
a.bp_hidden_from_external_users,
isnull(ba.bp_file,'') ba_file,  -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_id,'') ba_id, -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_size,'') ba_size,  -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_content_type,'') ba_content_type -- intentionally ba
from bug_posts a
left outer join users on us_id = a.bp_user
left outer join bug_posts ba on ba.bp_parent = a.bp_id and ba.bp_bug = a.bp_bug
where a.bp_bug = 71
and a.bp_parent is null
 and a.bp_type <> 'update'
 order by a.bp_id desc, ba.bp_parent, ba.bp_id

/* custom columns */ select sc.name, st.[name] [datatype], 
case when st.[name] = 'nvarchar' or st.[name] = 'nchar' then sc.length/2 else sc.length end as [length], 
sc.xprec, sc.xscale, sc.isnullable,
mm.text [default value], 
dflts.name [default name], 
isnull(ccm_dropdown_type,'') [dropdown type],
isnull(ccm_dropdown_vals,'') [vals],
isnull(ccm_sort_seq, sc.colorder) [column order],
sc.colorder
from syscolumns sc
inner join systypes st on st.xusertype = sc.xusertype
inner join sysobjects so on sc.id = so.id
left outer join syscomments mm on sc.cdefault = mm.id
left outer join custom_col_metadata on ccm_colorder = sc.colorder
left outer join sysobjects dflts on dflts.id = mm.id
where so.name = 'bugs'
and st.[name] <> 'sysname'
and sc.name not in ('rowguid',
'bg_id',
'bg_short_desc',
'bg_reported_user',
'bg_reported_date',
'bg_project',
'bg_org',
'bg_category',
'bg_priority',
'bg_status',
'bg_assigned_to_user',
'bg_last_updated_user',
'bg_last_updated_date',
'bg_user_defined_attribute',
'bg_project_custom_dropdown_value1',
'bg_project_custom_dropdown_value2',
'bg_project_custom_dropdown_value3',
'bg_tags')
order by sc.id, isnull(ccm_sort_seq,sc.colorder)

select
a.bp_bug,
a.bp_comment,
isnull(us_username,'') [us_username],
case rtrim(us_firstname)
	when null then isnull(us_lastname, '')
	when '' then isnull(us_lastname, '')

	end [us_fullname],
isnull(us_email,'') [us_email],
a.bp_date,
datediff(s,a.bp_date,getdate()) [seconds_ago],
a.bp_id,
a.bp_type,
isnull(a.bp_email_from,'') bp_email_from,
isnull(a.bp_email_to,'') bp_email_to,
isnull(a.bp_email_cc,'') bp_email_cc,
isnull(a.bp_file,'') bp_file,
isnull(a.bp_size,0) bp_size,
isnull(a.bp_content_type,'') bp_content_type,
a.bp_hidden_from_external_users,
isnull(ba.bp_file,'') ba_file,  -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_id,'') ba_id, -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_size,'') ba_size,  -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_content_type,'') ba_content_type -- intentionally ba
from bug_posts a
left outer join users on us_id = a.bp_user
left outer join bug_posts ba on ba.bp_parent = a.bp_id and ba.bp_bug = a.bp_bug
where a.bp_bug = 44
and a.bp_parent is null
 and a.bp_type <> 'update'
 order by a.bp_id desc, ba.bp_parent, ba.bp_id

 /* get_bug_datarow */
if not exists (select bu_bug from bug_user where bu_bug = 71 and bu_user = 16)
	insert into bug_user (bu_bug, bu_user, bu_flag, bu_seen, bu_vote) values(71, 16, 0, 1, 0) 
update bug_user set bu_seen = 1, bu_seen_datetime = getdate() where bu_bug = 71 and bu_user = 16 and bu_seen <> 1
declare @svn_revisions int
declare @git_commits int
declare @hg_revisions int
declare @tasks int
declare @related int;
set @svn_revisions = 0
set @git_commits = 0
set @hg_revisions = 0
set @tasks = 0
set @related = 0

select bg_id [id],
bg_short_desc [short_desc],
isnull(bg_tags,'') [bg_tags],
isnull(ru.us_username,'[deleted user]') [reporter],
isnull(ru.us_email,'') [reporter_email],
case rtrim(ru.us_firstname)

		and pu_permission_level = 0)

/* get_bug_posts */
select
a.bp_bug,
a.bp_comment,
isnull(us_username,'') [us_username],
case rtrim(us_firstname)
	when null then isnull(us_lastname, '')
	when '' then isnull(us_lastname, '')
	else isnull(us_lastname + ', ' + us_firstname,'')
	end [us_fullname],
isnull(us_email,'') [us_email],
a.bp_date,
datediff(s,a.bp_date,getdate()) [seconds_ago],
a.bp_id,
a.bp_type,
isnull(a.bp_email_from,'') bp_email_from,
isnull(a.bp_email_to,'') bp_email_to,
isnull(a.bp_email_cc,'') bp_email_cc,
isnull(a.bp_file,'') bp_file,
isnull(a.bp_size,0) bp_size,
isnull(a.bp_content_type,'') bp_content_type,
a.bp_hidden_from_external_users,
isnull(ba.bp_file,'') ba_file,  -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_id,'') ba_id, -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_size,'') ba_size,  -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_content_type,'') ba_content_type -- intentionally ba
from bug_posts a
left outer join users on us_id = a.bp_user
left outer join bug_posts ba on ba.bp_parent = a.bp_id and ba.bp_bug = a.bp_bug
where a.bp_bug = 71
and a.bp_parent is null
 and a.bp_type <> 'update'
 order by a.bp_id desc, ba.bp_parent, ba.bp_id

declare @pj int
select @pj = bg_project from bugs where bg_id = 71

delete from bug_subscriptions
where bs_bug = 71
and bs_user in
(select x.pu_user
from projects
left outer join project_user_xref x on pu_project = pj_id
where pu_project = @pj
and isnull(pu_permission_level,2) = 0)

delete from bug_subscriptions
where bs_bug = 71
and bs_user in
(select us_id from users
 inner join orgs on us_org = og_id
 inner join bugs on bg_id = 71
 where og_other_orgs_permission_level = 0
 and bg_org <> og_id)

insert into bug_subscriptions (bs_bug, bs_user)
select 71, us_id
from users
inner join orgs on us_org = og_id
inner join bugs on bg_id = 71
left outer join project_user_xref on pu_project = @pj and pu_user = us_id
where us_auto_subscribe = 1
and
case
	when
		us_org <> bg_org
		and og_other_orgs_permission_level < 2
		and og_other_orgs_permission_level < isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
			then og_other_orgs_permission_level
	else
		isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
end <> 0
and us_active = 1
and us_id not in
(select bs_user from bug_subscriptions
where bs_bug = 71)

insert into bug_subscriptions (bs_bug, bs_user)
select 71, pj_default_user
from projects
inner join users on pj_default_user = us_id
where pj_id = @pj
and pj_default_user <> 0
and pj_auto_subscribe_default_user = 1
and us_active = 1
and pj_default_user not in
(select bs_user from bug_subscriptions
where bs_bug = 71)

	else
		isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
end <> 0
and us_active = 1
and pu_project = @pj
and pu_user not in
(select bs_user from bug_subscriptions
where bs_bug = 71)

/* get notification emails for all subscribers */
select us_email, us_id, us_admin, og.*
from bug_subscriptions
inner join users on bs_user = us_id
inner join orgs og on us_org = og_id
inner join bugs on bg_id = bs_bug
left outer join project_user_xref on pu_user = us_id and pu_project = bg_project
where us_email is not null
and us_enable_notifications = 1
-- $status_change
and us_active = 1
and us_email <> ''
and (   (2 <= us_reported_notifications and bg_reported_user = bs_user)
or (2 <= us_assigned_notifications and bg_assigned_to_user = bs_user)
or (2 <= us_assigned_notifications and 16 = bs_user)
or (2 <= us_subscribed_notifications))
and
case
when
us_org <> bg_org
and og_other_orgs_permission_level < 2
and og_other_orgs_permission_level < isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
	then og_other_orgs_permission_level
else
isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
end <> 0
and bs_bug = 71
and (us_id <> 16 or isnull(us_send_notifications_to_self,0) = 1)

'bg_project_custom_dropdown_value3',
'bg_tags')
and st.[name] in ('nvarchar','varchar')
and sc.length > 30

	when null then isnull(ru.us_lastname, '')
	when '' then isnull(ru.us_lastname, '')
	else isnull(ru.us_lastname + ', ' + ru.us_firstname,'')
	end [reporter_fullname],

	when null then isnull(lu.us_lastname, '')
	when '' then isnull(lu.us_lastname, '')
	else isnull(lu.us_lastname + ', ' + lu.us_firstname,'')
	end [last_updated_fullname],


bg_last_updated_date [last_updated_date],
isnull(bg_project,0) [project],
isnull(pj_name,'[no project]') [current_project],

isnull(ct_name,'') [category_name],

isnull(st_name,'') [status_name],

when '' then isnull(asg.us_lastname, '[not assigned]')
else isnull(asg.us_lastname + ', ' + asg.us_firstname,'[not assigned]')
end [assigned_to_fullname],

isnull(bs_user,0) [subscribed],

case
when
	1 <> bg_org
	and userorg.og_other_orgs_permission_level < 2
	and userorg.og_other_orgs_permission_level < isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
		then userorg.og_other_orgs_permission_level
else
	isnull(pu_permission_level,2)

@tasks [task_cnt],
getdate() [snapshot_timestamp]

	(select pu_user from project_user_xref
		where pu_project = 11
		and pu_permission_level = 0)
order by us_username;

select
a.bp_bug,
a.bp_comment,
isnull(us_username,'') [us_username],
case rtrim(us_firstname)
	when null then isnull(us_lastname, '')
	when '' then isnull(us_lastname, '')
	else isnull(us_lastname + ', ' + us_firstname,'')
	end [us_fullname],
isnull(us_email,'') [us_email],
a.bp_date,
datediff(s,a.bp_date,getdate()) [seconds_ago],
a.bp_id,
a.bp_type,
isnull(a.bp_email_from,'') bp_email_from,
isnull(a.bp_email_to,'') bp_email_to,
isnull(a.bp_email_cc,'') bp_email_cc,
isnull(a.bp_file,'') bp_file,
isnull(a.bp_size,0) bp_size,
isnull(a.bp_content_type,'') bp_content_type,
a.bp_hidden_from_external_users,
isnull(ba.bp_file,'') ba_file,  -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_id,'') ba_id, -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_size,'') ba_size,  -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_content_type,'') ba_content_type -- intentionally ba
from bug_posts a
left outer join users on us_id = a.bp_user
left outer join bug_posts ba on ba.bp_parent = a.bp_id and ba.bp_bug = a.bp_bug
where a.bp_bug = 90
and a.bp_parent is null
 and a.bp_type <> 'update'
 order by a.bp_id desc, ba.bp_parent, ba.bp_id

 /* get_bug_datarow */
if not exists (select bu_bug from bug_user where bu_bug = 78 and bu_user = 16)
	insert into bug_user (bu_bug, bu_user, bu_flag, bu_seen, bu_vote) values(78, 16, 0, 1, 0) 
update bug_user set bu_seen = 1, bu_seen_datetime = getdate() where bu_bug = 78 and bu_user = 16 and bu_seen <> 1
declare @svn_revisions int
declare @git_commits int
declare @hg_revisions int
declare @tasks int
declare @related int;
set @svn_revisions = 0
set @git_commits = 0
set @hg_revisions = 0
set @tasks = 0
set @related = 0

select bg_id [id],
bg_short_desc [short_desc],
isnull(bg_tags,'') [bg_tags],
isnull(ru.us_username,'[deleted user]') [reporter],
isnull(ru.us_email,'') [reporter_email],
case rtrim(ru.us_firstname)
	when null then isnull(ru.us_lastname, '')
	when '' then isnull(ru.us_lastname, '')
	else isnull(ru.us_lastname + ', ' + ru.us_firstname,'')
	end [reporter_fullname],
bg_reported_date [reported_date],
datediff(s,bg_reported_date,getdate()) [seconds_ago],
isnull(lu.us_username,'') [last_updated_user],
case rtrim(lu.us_firstname)
	when null then isnull(lu.us_lastname, '')
	when '' then isnull(lu.us_lastname, '')
	else isnull(lu.us_lastname + ', ' + lu.us_firstname,'')
	end [last_updated_fullname],


bg_last_updated_date [last_updated_date],
isnull(bg_project,0) [project],
isnull(pj_name,'[no project]') [current_project],

isnull(bg_org,0) [organization],
isnull(bugorg.og_name,'') [og_name],

isnull(bg_category,0) [category],
isnull(ct_name,'') [category_name],

isnull(bg_priority,0) [priority],
isnull(pr_name,'') [priority_name],

isnull(bg_status,0) [status],
isnull(st_name,'') [status_name],

isnull(bg_user_defined_attribute,0) [udf],
isnull(udf_name,'') [udf_name],

isnull(bg_assigned_to_user,0) [assigned_to_user],
isnull(asg.us_username,'[not assigned]') [assigned_to_username],
case rtrim(asg.us_firstname)
when null then isnull(asg.us_lastname, '[not assigned]')
when '' then isnull(asg.us_lastname, '[not assigned]')
else isnull(asg.us_lastname + ', ' + asg.us_firstname,'[not assigned]')
end [assigned_to_fullname],

isnull(bs_user,0) [subscribed],

case
when
	1 <> bg_org
	and userorg.og_other_orgs_permission_level < 2
	and userorg.og_other_orgs_permission_level < isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
		then userorg.og_other_orgs_permission_level
else
	isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
end [pu_permission_level],

isnull(bg_project_custom_dropdown_value1,'') [bg_project_custom_dropdown_value1],
isnull(bg_project_custom_dropdown_value2,'') [bg_project_custom_dropdown_value2],
isnull(bg_project_custom_dropdown_value3,'') [bg_project_custom_dropdown_value3],
@related [relationship_cnt],
@svn_revisions [svn_revision_cnt],
@git_commits [git_commit_cnt],
@hg_revisions [hg_commit_cnt],
@tasks [task_cnt],
getdate() [snapshot_timestamp]

from bugs
inner join users this_user on us_id = 16
inner join orgs userorg on this_user.us_org = userorg.og_id
left outer join user_defined_attribute on bg_user_defined_attribute = udf_id
left outer join projects on bg_project = pj_id
left outer join orgs bugorg on bg_org = bugorg.og_id
left outer join categories on bg_category = ct_id
left outer join priorities on bg_priority = pr_id
left outer join statuses on bg_status = st_id
left outer join users asg on bg_assigned_to_user = asg.us_id
left outer join users ru on bg_reported_user = ru.us_id
left outer join users lu on bg_last_updated_user = lu.us_id
left outer join bug_subscriptions on bs_bug = bg_id and bs_user = 16
left outer join project_user_xref on pj_id = pu_project
and pu_user = 16
where bg_id = 78

/* drop downs */ select pj_id, pj_name
		from projects
		left outer join project_user_xref on pj_id = pu_project
		and pu_user = 16
		where pj_active = 1
		and isnull(pu_permission_level,2) not in (0, 1)
		order by pj_name;
select og_id, og_name from orgs where og_active = 1 order by og_name;
select ct_id, ct_name from categories order by ct_sort_seq, ct_name;

/* get_bug_posts */
select
a.bp_bug,
a.bp_comment,
isnull(us_username,'') [us_username],
case rtrim(us_firstname)
	when null then isnull(us_lastname, '')
	when '' then isnull(us_lastname, '')
	else isnull(us_lastname + ', ' + us_firstname,'')
	end [us_fullname],
isnull(us_email,'') [us_email],
a.bp_date,
datediff(s,a.bp_date,getdate()) [seconds_ago],
a.bp_id,
a.bp_type,
isnull(a.bp_email_from,'') bp_email_from,
isnull(a.bp_email_to,'') bp_email_to,
isnull(a.bp_email_cc,'') bp_email_cc,
isnull(a.bp_file,'') bp_file,
isnull(a.bp_size,0) bp_size,
isnull(a.bp_content_type,'') bp_content_type,
a.bp_hidden_from_external_users,
isnull(ba.bp_file,'') ba_file,  -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_id,'') ba_id, -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_size,'') ba_size,  -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_content_type,'') ba_content_type -- intentionally ba
from bug_posts a
left outer join users on us_id = a.bp_user
left outer join bug_posts ba on ba.bp_parent = a.bp_id and ba.bp_bug = a.bp_bug
where a.bp_bug = 78
and a.bp_parent is null
 and a.bp_type <> 'update'
 order by a.bp_id desc, ba.bp_parent, ba.bp_id

declare @pj int

delete from bug_subscriptions
where bs_bug = 78
and bs_user in
(select x.pu_user
from projects
left outer join project_user_xref x on pu_project = pj_id
where pu_project = @pj
and isnull(pu_permission_level,2) = 0)

delete from bug_subscriptions
where bs_bug = 78
and bs_user in
(select us_id from users
 inner join orgs on us_org = og_id
 inner join bugs on bg_id = 78
 where og_other_orgs_permission_level = 0
 and bg_org <> og_id)

insert into bug_subscriptions (bs_bug, bs_user)
select 78, us_id
from users
inner join orgs on us_org = og_id
inner join bugs on bg_id = 78
left outer join project_user_xref on pu_project = @pj and pu_user = us_id
where us_auto_subscribe = 1
and
case
	when
		us_org <> bg_org
		and og_other_orgs_permission_level < 2
		and og_other_orgs_permission_level < isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
			then og_other_orgs_permission_level
	else
		isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
end <> 0
and us_active = 1
and us_id not in
(select bs_user from bug_subscriptions
where bs_bug = 78)

/* get notification emails for all subscribers */
select us_email, us_id, us_admin, og.*
from bug_subscriptions
inner join users on bs_user = us_id
inner join orgs og on us_org = og_id
inner join bugs on bg_id = bs_bug
left outer join project_user_xref on pu_user = us_id and pu_project = bg_project
where us_email is not null
and us_enable_notifications = 1
-- $status_change
and us_active = 1
and us_email <> ''
and (   (2 <= us_reported_notifications and bg_reported_user = bs_user)
or (2 <= us_assigned_notifications and bg_assigned_to_user = bs_user)
or (2 <= us_assigned_notifications and 16 = bs_user)
or (2 <= us_subscribed_notifications))
and
case
when
us_org <> bg_org
and og_other_orgs_permission_level < 2
and og_other_orgs_permission_level < isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
	then og_other_orgs_permission_level
else
isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
end <> 0
and bs_bug = 78
and (us_id <> 16 or isnull(us_send_notifications_to_self,0) = 1)

/* get searchable cols */					
select sc.name
from syscolumns sc
inner join systypes st on st.xusertype = sc.xusertype
inner join sysobjects so on sc.id = so.id
where so.name = 'bugs'
and st.[name] <> 'sysname'
and sc.name not in ('rowguid',
'bg_id',
'bg_short_desc',
'bg_reported_user',
'bg_reported_date',
'bg_project',
'bg_org',
'bg_category',
'bg_priority',
'bg_status',
'bg_assigned_to_user',
'bg_last_updated_user',
'bg_last_updated_date',
'bg_user_defined_attribute',
'bg_project_custom_dropdown_value1',
'bg_project_custom_dropdown_value2',
'bg_project_custom_dropdown_value3',
'bg_tags')
and st.[name] in ('nvarchar','varchar')

/* check session */
declare @project_admin int
select @project_admin = count(1)
	from sessions
	inner join project_user_xref on pu_user = se_user
	and pu_admin = 1
	where se_id = '16088cb5-2541-4c37-9f16-89c13bbfe945';

select us_id, us_admin,
us_username, us_firstname, us_lastname,
isnull(us_email,'') us_email,
isnull(us_bugs_per_page,10) us_bugs_per_page,
isnull(us_forced_project,0) us_forced_project,
us_use_fckeditor,
us_enable_bug_list_popups,
og.*,
isnull(us_forced_project, 0 ) us_forced_project,
isnull(pu_permission_level, 2) pu_permission_level,
@project_admin [project_admin]
from sessions
inner join users on se_user = us_id
inner join orgs og on us_org = og_id
left outer join project_user_xref
	on pu_project = us_forced_project
	and pu_user = us_id
where se_id = '16088cb5-2541-4c37-9f16-89c13bbfe945'
and us_active = 1

/* get_bug_posts */
select
a.bp_bug,
a.bp_comment,
isnull(us_username,'') [us_username],
case rtrim(us_firstname)
	when null then isnull(us_lastname, '')
	when '' then isnull(us_lastname, '')
	else isnull(us_lastname + ', ' + us_firstname,'')
	end [us_fullname],
isnull(us_email,'') [us_email],
a.bp_date,
datediff(s,a.bp_date,getdate()) [seconds_ago],
a.bp_id,
a.bp_type,
isnull(a.bp_email_from,'') bp_email_from,
isnull(a.bp_email_to,'') bp_email_to,
isnull(a.bp_email_cc,'') bp_email_cc,
isnull(a.bp_file,'') bp_file,
isnull(a.bp_size,0) bp_size,
isnull(a.bp_content_type,'') bp_content_type,
a.bp_hidden_from_external_users,
isnull(ba.bp_file,'') ba_file,  -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_id,'') ba_id, -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_size,'') ba_size,  -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_content_type,'') ba_content_type -- intentionally ba
from bug_posts a
left outer join users on us_id = a.bp_user
left outer join bug_posts ba on ba.bp_parent = a.bp_id and ba.bp_bug = a.bp_bug
where a.bp_bug = 44
and a.bp_parent is null
 and a.bp_type <> 'update'
 order by a.bp_id desc, ba.bp_parent, ba.bp_id
2016-01-04 04:07:00 http://learncodinganywhere.com/bugtracker/ajax.aspx?bugid=44 elapsed milliseconds:0000
2016-01-04 04:07:00 http://learncodinganywhere.com/bugtracker/ajax.aspx?bugid=79 sql=

	else isnull(lu.us_lastname + ', ' + lu.us_firstname,'')
	end [last_updated_fullname],

when '' then isnull(asg.us_lastname, '[not assigned]')
else isnull(asg.us_lastname + ', ' + asg.us_firstname,'[not assigned]')
end [assigned_to_fullname],

case
when
	1 <> bg_org
	and userorg.og_other_orgs_permission_level < 2
	and userorg.og_other_orgs_permission_level < isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
		then userorg.og_other_orgs_permission_level
else
	isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
end [pu_permission_level],

isnull(bg_project_custom_dropdown_value1,'') [bg_project_custom_dropdown_value1],
isnull(bg_project_custom_dropdown_value2,'') [bg_project_custom_dropdown_value2],

@related [relationship_cnt],

@git_commits [git_commit_cnt],
@hg_revisions [hg_commit_cnt],
@tasks [task_cnt],
getdate() [snapshot_timestamp]

from bugs
inner join users this_user on us_id = 16
inner join orgs userorg on this_user.us_org = userorg.og_id
left outer join user_defined_attribute on bg_user_defined_attribute = udf_id
left outer join projects on bg_project = pj_id
left outer join orgs bugorg on bg_org = bugorg.og_id
left outer join categories on bg_category = ct_id
left outer join priorities on bg_priority = pr_id
left outer join statuses on bg_status = st_id
left outer join users asg on bg_assigned_to_user = asg.us_id
left outer join users ru on bg_reported_user = ru.us_id
left outer join users lu on bg_last_updated_user = lu.us_id
left outer join bug_subscriptions on bs_bug = bg_id and bs_user = 16
left outer join project_user_xref on pj_id = pu_project
and pu_user = 16
where bg_id = 44

/* drop downs */ select pj_id, pj_name
		from projects
		left outer join project_user_xref on pj_id = pu_project

		order by pj_name;
select og_id, og_name from orgs where og_active = 1 order by og_name;
select ct_id, ct_name from categories order by ct_sort_seq, ct_name;
select pr_id, pr_name from priorities order by pr_sort_seq, pr_name;
select st_id, st_name from statuses order by st_sort_seq, st_name;
select udf_id, udf_name from user_defined_attribute order by udf_sort_seq, udf_name;

/* users this project */ select us_id, case when 0 = 1 then us_lastname + ', ' + us_firstname else us_username end us_username

and og_can_be_assigned_to = 1
and (2 <> 0 or 1 = og_id or (og_external_user = 0 and 0 = 1))
and us_id not in
	(select pu_user from project_user_xref
		where pu_project = 11
		and pu_permission_level = 0)
order by us_username;

/* get_bug_posts */
select
a.bp_bug,
a.bp_comment,
isnull(us_username,'') [us_username],
case rtrim(us_firstname)
	when null then isnull(us_lastname, '')
	when '' then isnull(us_lastname, '')
	else isnull(us_lastname + ', ' + us_firstname,'')
	end [us_fullname],
isnull(us_email,'') [us_email],
a.bp_date,
datediff(s,a.bp_date,getdate()) [seconds_ago],
a.bp_id,
a.bp_type,
isnull(a.bp_email_from,'') bp_email_from,
isnull(a.bp_email_to,'') bp_email_to,
isnull(a.bp_email_cc,'') bp_email_cc,
isnull(a.bp_file,'') bp_file,
isnull(a.bp_size,0) bp_size,
isnull(a.bp_content_type,'') bp_content_type,
a.bp_hidden_from_external_users,
isnull(ba.bp_file,'') ba_file,  -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_id,'') ba_id, -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_size,'') ba_size,  -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_content_type,'') ba_content_type -- intentionally ba
from bug_posts a
left outer join users on us_id = a.bp_user
left outer join bug_posts ba on ba.bp_parent = a.bp_id and ba.bp_bug = a.bp_bug
where a.bp_bug = 94
and a.bp_parent is null
 and a.bp_type <> 'update'
 order by a.bp_id desc, ba.bp_parent, ba.bp_id

/* get notification emails for all subscribers */
select us_email, us_id, us_admin, og.*
from bug_subscriptions
inner join users on bs_user = us_id
inner join orgs og on us_org = og_id
inner join bugs on bg_id = bs_bug
left outer join project_user_xref on pu_user = us_id and pu_project = bg_project
where us_email is not null
and us_enable_notifications = 1
-- $status_change
and us_active = 1
and us_email <> ''
and (   (2 <= us_reported_notifications and bg_reported_user = bs_user)
or (2 <= us_assigned_notifications and bg_assigned_to_user = bs_user)
or (2 <= us_assigned_notifications and 16 = bs_user)
or (2 <= us_subscribed_notifications))
and
case
when
us_org <> bg_org
and og_other_orgs_permission_level < 2
and og_other_orgs_permission_level < isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
	then og_other_orgs_permission_level
else
isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
end <> 0
and bs_bug = 44
and (us_id <> 16 or isnull(us_send_notifications_to_self,0) = 1)

select
a.bp_bug,
a.bp_comment,
isnull(us_username,'') [us_username],
case rtrim(us_firstname)
	when null then isnull(us_lastname, '')
	when '' then isnull(us_lastname, '')
	else isnull(us_lastname + ', ' + us_firstname,'')
	end [us_fullname],
isnull(us_email,'') [us_email],
a.bp_date,
datediff(s,a.bp_date,getdate()) [seconds_ago],
a.bp_id,
a.bp_type,
isnull(a.bp_email_from,'') bp_email_from,
isnull(a.bp_email_to,'') bp_email_to,
isnull(a.bp_email_cc,'') bp_email_cc,
isnull(a.bp_file,'') bp_file,
isnull(a.bp_size,0) bp_size,
isnull(a.bp_content_type,'') bp_content_type,
a.bp_hidden_from_external_users,
isnull(ba.bp_file,'') ba_file,  -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_id,'') ba_id, -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_size,'') ba_size,  -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_content_type,'') ba_content_type -- intentionally ba
from bug_posts a
left outer join users on us_id = a.bp_user
left outer join bug_posts ba on ba.bp_parent = a.bp_id and ba.bp_bug = a.bp_bug
where a.bp_bug = 44
and a.bp_parent is null
 order by a.bp_id desc, ba.bp_parent, ba.bp_id

	when '' then isnull(lu.us_lastname, '')
	else isnull(lu.us_lastname + ', ' + lu.us_firstname,'')
	end [last_updated_fullname],

	(select pu_user from project_user_xref
		where pu_project = 11
		and pu_permission_level = 0)
order by us_username;

/* get_bug_posts */
select
a.bp_bug,
a.bp_comment,
isnull(us_username,'') [us_username],
case rtrim(us_firstname)
	when null then isnull(us_lastname, '')
	when '' then isnull(us_lastname, '')
	else isnull(us_lastname + ', ' + us_firstname,'')
	end [us_fullname],
isnull(us_email,'') [us_email],
a.bp_date,
datediff(s,a.bp_date,getdate()) [seconds_ago],
a.bp_id,
a.bp_type,
isnull(a.bp_email_from,'') bp_email_from,
isnull(a.bp_email_to,'') bp_email_to,
isnull(a.bp_email_cc,'') bp_email_cc,
isnull(a.bp_file,'') bp_file,
isnull(a.bp_size,0) bp_size,
isnull(a.bp_content_type,'') bp_content_type,
a.bp_hidden_from_external_users,
isnull(ba.bp_file,'') ba_file,  -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_id,'') ba_id, -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_size,'') ba_size,  -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_content_type,'') ba_content_type -- intentionally ba
from bug_posts a
left outer join users on us_id = a.bp_user
left outer join bug_posts ba on ba.bp_parent = a.bp_id and ba.bp_bug = a.bp_bug
where a.bp_bug = 59
and a.bp_parent is null
 and a.bp_type <> 'update'
 order by a.bp_id desc, ba.bp_parent, ba.bp_id

isnull(us_email,'') us_email,
isnull(us_bugs_per_page,10) us_bugs_per_page,
isnull(us_forced_project,0) us_forced_project,
us_use_fckeditor,
us_enable_bug_list_popups,
og.*,
isnull(us_forced_project, 0 ) us_forced_project,
isnull(pu_permission_level, 2) pu_permission_level,
@project_admin [project_admin]
from sessions
inner join users on se_user = us_id
inner join orgs og on us_org = og_id

	on pu_project = us_forced_project
	and pu_user = us_id

and us_active = 1

/* get_bug_posts */
select
a.bp_bug,
a.bp_comment,
isnull(us_username,'') [us_username],
case rtrim(us_firstname)
	when null then isnull(us_lastname, '')
	when '' then isnull(us_lastname, '')
	else isnull(us_lastname + ', ' + us_firstname,'')
	end [us_fullname],
isnull(us_email,'') [us_email],
a.bp_date,
datediff(s,a.bp_date,getdate()) [seconds_ago],
a.bp_id,
a.bp_type,
isnull(a.bp_email_from,'') bp_email_from,
isnull(a.bp_email_to,'') bp_email_to,
isnull(a.bp_email_cc,'') bp_email_cc,
isnull(a.bp_file,'') bp_file,
isnull(a.bp_size,0) bp_size,
isnull(a.bp_content_type,'') bp_content_type,
a.bp_hidden_from_external_users,
isnull(ba.bp_file,'') ba_file,  -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_id,'') ba_id, -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_size,'') ba_size,  -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_content_type,'') ba_content_type -- intentionally ba
from bug_posts a
left outer join users on us_id = a.bp_user
left outer join bug_posts ba on ba.bp_parent = a.bp_id and ba.bp_bug = a.bp_bug
where a.bp_bug = 45
and a.bp_parent is null
 and a.bp_type <> 'update'
 order by a.bp_id desc, ba.bp_parent, ba.bp_id
2016-01-04 16:53:28 http://learncodinganywhere.com/bugtracker/ajax.aspx?bugid=45 elapsed milliseconds:0000
2016-01-04 17:02:49 http://learncodinganywhere.com/bugtracker/ajax.aspx?bugid=85 sql=

declare @pj int
select @pj = bg_project from bugs where bg_id = 110

delete from bug_subscriptions
where bs_bug = 110
and bs_user in
(select x.pu_user
from projects
left outer join project_user_xref x on pu_project = pj_id
where pu_project = @pj
and isnull(pu_permission_level,2) = 0)

delete from bug_subscriptions
where bs_bug = 110
and bs_user in
(select us_id from users
 inner join orgs on us_org = og_id
 inner join bugs on bg_id = 110
 where og_other_orgs_permission_level = 0
 and bg_org <> og_id)

insert into bug_subscriptions (bs_bug, bs_user)
select 110, us_id
from users
inner join orgs on us_org = og_id
inner join bugs on bg_id = 110
left outer join project_user_xref on pu_project = @pj and pu_user = us_id
where us_auto_subscribe = 1
and
case
	when
		us_org <> bg_org
		and og_other_orgs_permission_level < 2
		and og_other_orgs_permission_level < isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
			then og_other_orgs_permission_level
	else
		isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
end <> 0
and us_active = 1
and us_id not in
(select bs_user from bug_subscriptions
where bs_bug = 110)

from projects

where pj_id = @pj
and pj_default_user <> 0
and pj_auto_subscribe_default_user = 1
and us_active = 1
and pj_default_user not in
(select bs_user from bug_subscriptions
where bs_bug = 110)

	else
		isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
end <> 0
and us_active = 1

/* get notification emails for all subscribers */
select us_email, us_id, us_admin, og.*
from bug_subscriptions
inner join users on bs_user = us_id
inner join orgs og on us_org = og_id
inner join bugs on bg_id = bs_bug
left outer join project_user_xref on pu_user = us_id and pu_project = bg_project
where us_email is not null
and us_enable_notifications = 1
-- $status_change
and us_active = 1
and us_email <> ''
and (   (1 <= us_reported_notifications and bg_reported_user = bs_user)
or (1 <= us_assigned_notifications and bg_assigned_to_user = bs_user)
or (1 <= us_assigned_notifications and 0 = bs_user)
or (1 <= us_subscribed_notifications))
and
case
when
us_org <> bg_org
and og_other_orgs_permission_level < 2
and og_other_orgs_permission_level < isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
	then og_other_orgs_permission_level
else
isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
end <> 0
and bs_bug = 110
and (us_id <> 15 or isnull(us_send_notifications_to_self,0) = 1)

/* get searchable cols */

from syscolumns sc
inner join systypes st on st.xusertype = sc.xusertype
inner join sysobjects so on sc.id = so.id

and st.[name] <> 'sysname'
and sc.name not in ('rowguid',
'bg_id',
'bg_short_desc',
'bg_reported_user',
'bg_reported_date',

'bg_org',
'bg_category',

'bg_user_defined_attribute',
'bg_project_custom_dropdown_value1',
'bg_project_custom_dropdown_value2',
'bg_project_custom_dropdown_value3',
'bg_tags')
and st.[name] in ('nvarchar','varchar')
and sc.length > 30

/* get_bug_posts */
select
a.bp_bug,
a.bp_comment,
isnull(us_username,'') [us_username],
case rtrim(us_firstname)
	when null then isnull(us_lastname, '')
	when '' then isnull(us_lastname, '')
	else isnull(us_lastname + ', ' + us_firstname,'')
	end [us_fullname],
isnull(us_email,'') [us_email],
a.bp_date,
datediff(s,a.bp_date,getdate()) [seconds_ago],
a.bp_id,
a.bp_type,
isnull(a.bp_email_from,'') bp_email_from,
isnull(a.bp_email_to,'') bp_email_to,
isnull(a.bp_email_cc,'') bp_email_cc,
isnull(a.bp_file,'') bp_file,
isnull(a.bp_size,0) bp_size,
isnull(a.bp_content_type,'') bp_content_type,
a.bp_hidden_from_external_users,
isnull(ba.bp_file,'') ba_file,  -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_id,'') ba_id, -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_size,'') ba_size,  -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_content_type,'') ba_content_type -- intentionally ba
from bug_posts a
left outer join users on us_id = a.bp_user
left outer join bug_posts ba on ba.bp_parent = a.bp_id and ba.bp_bug = a.bp_bug
where a.bp_bug = 110
and a.bp_parent is null
 order by a.bp_id desc, ba.bp_parent, ba.bp_id

	end [reporter_fullname],
bg_reported_date [reported_date],
datediff(s,bg_reported_date,getdate()) [seconds_ago],
isnull(lu.us_username,'') [last_updated_user],
case rtrim(lu.us_firstname)
	when null then isnull(lu.us_lastname, '')
	when '' then isnull(lu.us_lastname, '')
	else isnull(lu.us_lastname + ', ' + lu.us_firstname,'')
	end [last_updated_fullname],


bg_last_updated_date [last_updated_date],
isnull(bg_project,0) [project],
isnull(pj_name,'[no project]') [current_project],

isnull(bg_org,0) [organization],
isnull(bugorg.og_name,'') [og_name],

isnull(bg_category,0) [category],
isnull(ct_name,'') [category_name],

when '' then isnull(asg.us_lastname, '[not assigned]')
else isnull(asg.us_lastname + ', ' + asg.us_firstname,'[not assigned]')
end [assigned_to_fullname],

isnull(bs_user,0) [subscribed],

	1 <> bg_org
	and userorg.og_other_orgs_permission_level < 2
	and userorg.og_other_orgs_permission_level < isnull(pu_permission_level,2)

else
	isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
end [pu_permission_level],

@git_commits [git_commit_cnt],
@hg_revisions [hg_commit_cnt],
@tasks [task_cnt],
getdate() [snapshot_timestamp]

from bugs
inner join users this_user on us_id = 15
inner join orgs userorg on this_user.us_org = userorg.og_id
left outer join user_defined_attribute on bg_user_defined_attribute = udf_id
left outer join projects on bg_project = pj_id
left outer join orgs bugorg on bg_org = bugorg.og_id
left outer join categories on bg_category = ct_id
left outer join priorities on bg_priority = pr_id
left outer join statuses on bg_status = st_id
left outer join users asg on bg_assigned_to_user = asg.us_id
left outer join users ru on bg_reported_user = ru.us_id
left outer join users lu on bg_last_updated_user = lu.us_id
left outer join bug_subscriptions on bs_bug = bg_id and bs_user = 15
left outer join project_user_xref on pj_id = pu_project
and pu_user = 15
where bg_id = 110

 /* get_bug_datarow */
if not exists (select bu_bug from bug_user where bu_bug = 94 and bu_user = 15)
	insert into bug_user (bu_bug, bu_user, bu_flag, bu_seen, bu_vote) values(94, 15, 0, 1, 0) 
update bug_user set bu_seen = 1, bu_seen_datetime = getdate() where bu_bug = 94 and bu_user = 15 and bu_seen <> 1
declare @svn_revisions int
declare @git_commits int
declare @hg_revisions int
declare @tasks int
declare @related int;
set @svn_revisions = 0
set @git_commits = 0
set @hg_revisions = 0
set @tasks = 0
set @related = 0

select bg_id [id],
bg_short_desc [short_desc],
isnull(bg_tags,'') [bg_tags],
isnull(ru.us_username,'[deleted user]') [reporter],
isnull(ru.us_email,'') [reporter_email],
case rtrim(ru.us_firstname)
	when null then isnull(ru.us_lastname, '')
	when '' then isnull(ru.us_lastname, '')
	else isnull(ru.us_lastname + ', ' + ru.us_firstname,'')
	end [reporter_fullname],
bg_reported_date [reported_date],
datediff(s,bg_reported_date,getdate()) [seconds_ago],
isnull(lu.us_username,'') [last_updated_user],
case rtrim(lu.us_firstname)
	when null then isnull(lu.us_lastname, '')
	when '' then isnull(lu.us_lastname, '')
	else isnull(lu.us_lastname + ', ' + lu.us_firstname,'')
	end [last_updated_fullname],


bg_last_updated_date [last_updated_date],
isnull(bg_project,0) [project],
isnull(pj_name,'[no project]') [current_project],

when null then isnull(asg.us_lastname, '[not assigned]')
when '' then isnull(asg.us_lastname, '[not assigned]')
else isnull(asg.us_lastname + ', ' + asg.us_firstname,'[not assigned]')
end [assigned_to_fullname],

isnull(bs_user,0) [subscribed],

case
when
	1 <> bg_org
	and userorg.og_other_orgs_permission_level < 2
	and userorg.og_other_orgs_permission_level < isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
		then userorg.og_other_orgs_permission_level
else
	isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
end [pu_permission_level],

isnull(bg_project_custom_dropdown_value1,'') [bg_project_custom_dropdown_value1],
isnull(bg_project_custom_dropdown_value2,'') [bg_project_custom_dropdown_value2],

@svn_revisions [svn_revision_cnt],
@git_commits [git_commit_cnt],
@hg_revisions [hg_commit_cnt],
@tasks [task_cnt],
getdate() [snapshot_timestamp]

from bugs
inner join users this_user on us_id = 15
inner join orgs userorg on this_user.us_org = userorg.og_id
left outer join user_defined_attribute on bg_user_defined_attribute = udf_id
left outer join projects on bg_project = pj_id
left outer join orgs bugorg on bg_org = bugorg.og_id
left outer join categories on bg_category = ct_id
left outer join priorities on bg_priority = pr_id
left outer join statuses on bg_status = st_id
left outer join users asg on bg_assigned_to_user = asg.us_id
left outer join users ru on bg_reported_user = ru.us_id
left outer join users lu on bg_last_updated_user = lu.us_id
left outer join bug_subscriptions on bs_bug = bg_id and bs_user = 15
left outer join project_user_xref on pj_id = pu_project
and pu_user = 15
where bg_id = 94

and us_id not in
	(select pu_user from project_user_xref
		where pu_project = 11
		and pu_permission_level = 0)
order by us_username;

a.bp_hidden_from_external_users,

isnull(ba.bp_content_type,'') ba_content_type -- intentionally ba

left outer join users on us_id = a.bp_user

and a.bp_parent is null
 and a.bp_type <> 'update'
 order by a.bp_id desc, ba.bp_parent, ba.bp_id

 bg_short_desc [desc], isnull(pj_name,'') [project], isnull(og_name,'') [organization], isnull(ct_name,'') [category], rpt.us_username [reported by],
 bg_reported_date [reported on], isnull(bu_seen,0) [$SEEN], isnull(pr_name,'') [priority], isnull(asg.us_username,'') [assigned to],

 /* get_bug_datarow */
if not exists (select bu_bug from bug_user where bu_bug = 45 and bu_user = 16)
	insert into bug_user (bu_bug, bu_user, bu_flag, bu_seen, bu_vote) values(45, 16, 0, 1, 0) 
update bug_user set bu_seen = 1, bu_seen_datetime = getdate() where bu_bug = 45 and bu_user = 16 and bu_seen <> 1
declare @svn_revisions int
declare @git_commits int
declare @hg_revisions int
declare @tasks int
declare @related int;
set @svn_revisions = 0
set @git_commits = 0
set @hg_revisions = 0
set @tasks = 0
set @related = 0

select bg_id [id],
bg_short_desc [short_desc],
isnull(bg_tags,'') [bg_tags],
isnull(ru.us_username,'[deleted user]') [reporter],
isnull(ru.us_email,'') [reporter_email],
case rtrim(ru.us_firstname)
	when null then isnull(ru.us_lastname, '')
	when '' then isnull(ru.us_lastname, '')
	else isnull(ru.us_lastname + ', ' + ru.us_firstname,'')
	end [reporter_fullname],
bg_reported_date [reported_date],
datediff(s,bg_reported_date,getdate()) [seconds_ago],
isnull(lu.us_username,'') [last_updated_user],
case rtrim(lu.us_firstname)
	when null then isnull(lu.us_lastname, '')
	when '' then isnull(lu.us_lastname, '')
	else isnull(lu.us_lastname + ', ' + lu.us_firstname,'')
	end [last_updated_fullname],


bg_last_updated_date [last_updated_date],
isnull(bg_project,0) [project],
isnull(pj_name,'[no project]') [current_project],

isnull(bg_org,0) [organization],
isnull(bugorg.og_name,'') [og_name],

isnull(bg_category,0) [category],
isnull(ct_name,'') [category_name],

isnull(bg_priority,0) [priority],
isnull(pr_name,'') [priority_name],

isnull(bg_status,0) [status],
isnull(st_name,'') [status_name],

isnull(bg_user_defined_attribute,0) [udf],
isnull(udf_name,'') [udf_name],

isnull(bg_assigned_to_user,0) [assigned_to_user],
isnull(asg.us_username,'[not assigned]') [assigned_to_username],
case rtrim(asg.us_firstname)
when null then isnull(asg.us_lastname, '[not assigned]')
when '' then isnull(asg.us_lastname, '[not assigned]')
else isnull(asg.us_lastname + ', ' + asg.us_firstname,'[not assigned]')
end [assigned_to_fullname],

isnull(bs_user,0) [subscribed],

case
when
	1 <> bg_org
	and userorg.og_other_orgs_permission_level < 2
	and userorg.og_other_orgs_permission_level < isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
		then userorg.og_other_orgs_permission_level
else
	isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
end [pu_permission_level],

isnull(bg_project_custom_dropdown_value1,'') [bg_project_custom_dropdown_value1],
isnull(bg_project_custom_dropdown_value2,'') [bg_project_custom_dropdown_value2],
isnull(bg_project_custom_dropdown_value3,'') [bg_project_custom_dropdown_value3],
@related [relationship_cnt],
@svn_revisions [svn_revision_cnt],
@git_commits [git_commit_cnt],
@hg_revisions [hg_commit_cnt],
@tasks [task_cnt],
getdate() [snapshot_timestamp]

from bugs
inner join users this_user on us_id = 16

/* users this project */ select us_id, case when 0 = 1 then us_lastname + ', ' + us_firstname else us_username end us_username
from users
inner join orgs on us_org = og_id
where us_active = 1
and og_can_be_assigned_to = 1
and (2 <> 0 or 1 = og_id or (og_external_user = 0 and 0 = 1))
and us_id not in
	(select pu_user from project_user_xref
		where pu_project = 11
		and pu_permission_level = 0)
order by us_username;

/* get_bug_posts */
select
a.bp_bug,
a.bp_comment,
isnull(us_username,'') [us_username],
case rtrim(us_firstname)
	when null then isnull(us_lastname, '')
	when '' then isnull(us_lastname, '')
	else isnull(us_lastname + ', ' + us_firstname,'')
	end [us_fullname],
isnull(us_email,'') [us_email],
a.bp_date,
datediff(s,a.bp_date,getdate()) [seconds_ago],
a.bp_id,
a.bp_type,
isnull(a.bp_email_from,'') bp_email_from,
isnull(a.bp_email_to,'') bp_email_to,
isnull(a.bp_email_cc,'') bp_email_cc,
isnull(a.bp_file,'') bp_file,
isnull(a.bp_size,0) bp_size,
isnull(a.bp_content_type,'') bp_content_type,
a.bp_hidden_from_external_users,
isnull(ba.bp_file,'') ba_file,  -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_id,'') ba_id, -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_size,'') ba_size,  -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_content_type,'') ba_content_type -- intentionally ba
from bug_posts a
left outer join users on us_id = a.bp_user
left outer join bug_posts ba on ba.bp_parent = a.bp_id and ba.bp_bug = a.bp_bug
where a.bp_bug = 45
and a.bp_parent is null
 and a.bp_type <> 'update'
 order by a.bp_id desc, ba.bp_parent, ba.bp_id

		declare @last_updated datetime
		select @last_updated = bg_last_updated_date from bugs where bg_id = 45
		if @last_updated > '20160104 23:04:16:933'
		begin
			-- signal that we did NOT do the update

declare @pj int
select @pj = bg_project from bugs where bg_id = 45

delete from bug_subscriptions
where bs_bug = 45
and bs_user in
(select x.pu_user
from projects
left outer join project_user_xref x on pu_project = pj_id
where pu_project = @pj
and isnull(pu_permission_level,2) = 0)

delete from bug_subscriptions
where bs_bug = 45
and bs_user in
(select us_id from users
 inner join orgs on us_org = og_id
 inner join bugs on bg_id = 45
 where og_other_orgs_permission_level = 0
 and bg_org <> og_id)

insert into bug_subscriptions (bs_bug, bs_user)
select 45, us_id
from users
inner join orgs on us_org = og_id
inner join bugs on bg_id = 45
left outer join project_user_xref on pu_project = @pj and pu_user = us_id
where us_auto_subscribe = 1
and
case
	when
		us_org <> bg_org
		and og_other_orgs_permission_level < 2
		and og_other_orgs_permission_level < isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
			then og_other_orgs_permission_level
	else
		isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
end <> 0
and us_active = 1
and us_id not in
(select bs_user from bug_subscriptions
where bs_bug = 45)

from projects
inner join users on pj_default_user = us_id
where pj_id = @pj
and pj_default_user <> 0
and pj_auto_subscribe_default_user = 1
and us_active = 1
and pj_default_user not in
(select bs_user from bug_subscriptions
where bs_bug = 45)

/* get notification emails for all subscribers */
select us_email, us_id, us_admin, og.*
from bug_subscriptions
inner join users on bs_user = us_id
inner join orgs og on us_org = og_id
inner join bugs on bg_id = bs_bug
left outer join project_user_xref on pu_user = us_id and pu_project = bg_project
where us_email is not null
and us_enable_notifications = 1
-- $status_change
and us_active = 1
and us_email <> ''
and (   (2 <= us_reported_notifications and bg_reported_user = bs_user)
or (2 <= us_assigned_notifications and bg_assigned_to_user = bs_user)
or (2 <= us_assigned_notifications and 16 = bs_user)
or (2 <= us_subscribed_notifications))
and
case
when
us_org <> bg_org
and og_other_orgs_permission_level < 2
and og_other_orgs_permission_level < isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
	then og_other_orgs_permission_level
else
isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
end <> 0
and bs_bug = 45
and (us_id <> 16 or isnull(us_send_notifications_to_self,0) = 1)

/* get searchable cols */					
select sc.name
from syscolumns sc
inner join systypes st on st.xusertype = sc.xusertype
inner join sysobjects so on sc.id = so.id
where so.name = 'bugs'
and st.[name] <> 'sysname'
and sc.name not in ('rowguid',
'bg_id',
'bg_short_desc',
'bg_reported_user',
'bg_reported_date',
'bg_project',
'bg_org',
'bg_category',
'bg_priority',

'bg_last_updated_user',

'bg_user_defined_attribute',
'bg_project_custom_dropdown_value1',
'bg_project_custom_dropdown_value2',
'bg_project_custom_dropdown_value3',
'bg_tags')
and st.[name] in ('nvarchar','varchar')
and sc.length > 30

select
a.bp_bug,
a.bp_comment,
isnull(us_username,'') [us_username],
case rtrim(us_firstname)
	when null then isnull(us_lastname, '')
	when '' then isnull(us_lastname, '')
	else isnull(us_lastname + ', ' + us_firstname,'')
	end [us_fullname],
isnull(us_email,'') [us_email],
a.bp_date,
datediff(s,a.bp_date,getdate()) [seconds_ago],
a.bp_id,
a.bp_type,
isnull(a.bp_email_from,'') bp_email_from,
isnull(a.bp_email_to,'') bp_email_to,
isnull(a.bp_email_cc,'') bp_email_cc,
isnull(a.bp_file,'') bp_file,
isnull(a.bp_size,0) bp_size,
isnull(a.bp_content_type,'') bp_content_type,
a.bp_hidden_from_external_users,
isnull(ba.bp_file,'') ba_file,  -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_id,'') ba_id, -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_size,'') ba_size,  -- intentionally ba
isnull(ba.bp_content_type,'') ba_content_type -- intentionally ba
from bug_posts a
left outer join users on us_id = a.bp_user
left outer join bug_posts ba on ba.bp_parent = a.bp_id and ba.bp_bug = a.bp_bug
where a.bp_bug = 52
and a.bp_parent is null
 and a.bp_type <> 'update'
 order by a.bp_id desc, ba.bp_parent, ba.bp_id

 /* get_bug_datarow */
if not exists (select bu_bug from bug_user where bu_bug = 59 and bu_user = 16)
	insert into bug_user (bu_bug, bu_user, bu_flag, bu_seen, bu_vote) values(59, 16, 0, 1, 0) 
update bug_user set bu_seen = 1, bu_seen_datetime = getdate() where bu_bug = 59 and bu_user = 16 and bu_seen <> 1
declare @svn_revisions int
declare @git_commits int
declare @hg_revisions int
declare @tasks int
declare @related int;
set @svn_revisions = 0
set @git_commits = 0
set @hg_revisions = 0
set @tasks = 0
set @related = 0

select bg_id [id],
bg_short_desc [short_desc],
isnull(bg_tags,'') [bg_tags],
isnull(ru.us_username,'[deleted user]') [reporter],
isnull(ru.us_email,'') [reporter_email],
case rtrim(ru.us_firstname)
	when null then isnull(ru.us_lastname, '')
	when '' then isnull(ru.us_lastname, '')
	else isnull(ru.us_lastname + ', ' + ru.us_firstname,'')
	end [reporter_fullname],
bg_reported_date [reported_date],
datediff(s,bg_reported_date,getdate()) [seconds_ago],
isnull(lu.us_username,'') [last_updated_user],
case rtrim(lu.us_firstname)
	when null then isnull(lu.us_lastname, '')
	when '' then isnull(lu.us_lastname, '')
	else isnull(lu.us_lastname + ', ' + lu.us_firstname,'')
	end [last_updated_fullname],


bg_last_updated_date [last_updated_date],
isnull(bg_project,0) [project],
isnull(pj_name,'[no project]') [current_project],

isnull(bg_org,0) [organization],
isnull(bugorg.og_name,'') [og_name],

isnull(bg_category,0) [category],
isnull(ct_name,'') [category_name],

isnull(bg_priority,0) [priority],
isnull(pr_name,'') [priority_name],

isnull(bg_status,0) [status],
isnull(st_name,'') [status_name],

isnull(bg_user_defined_attribute,0) [udf],
isnull(udf_name,'') [udf_name],

isnull(bg_assigned_to_user,0) [assigned_to_user],
isnull(asg.us_username,'[not assigned]') [assigned_to_username],
case rtrim(asg.us_firstname)
when null then isnull(asg.us_lastname, '[not assigned]')
when '' then isnull(asg.us_lastname, '[not assigned]')
else isnull(asg.us_lastname + ', ' + asg.us_firstname,'[not assigned]')
end [assigned_to_fullname],

isnull(bs_user,0) [subscribed],

case
when
	1 <> bg_org
	and userorg.og_other_orgs_permission_level < 2
	and userorg.og_other_orgs_permission_level < isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
		then userorg.og_other_orgs_permission_level
else
	isnull(pu_permission_level,2)
end [pu_permission_level],

isnull(bg_project_custom_dropdown_value1,'') [bg_project_custom_dropdown_value1],
isnull(bg_project_custom_dropdown_value2,'') [bg_project_custom_dropdown_value2],
isnull(bg_project_custom_dropdown_value3,'') [bg_project_custom_dropdown_value3],
@related [relationship_cnt],
@svn_revisions [svn_revision_cnt],
@git_commits [git_commit_cnt],
@hg_revisions [hg_commit_cnt],
@tasks [task_cnt],
getdate() [snapshot_timestamp]

from bugs
inner join users this_user on us_id = 16
inner join orgs userorg on this_user.us_org = userorg.og_id
left outer join user_defined_attribute on bg_user_defined_attribute = udf_id
left outer join projects on bg_project = pj_id
left outer join orgs bugorg on bg_org = bugorg.og_id
left outer join categories on bg_category = ct_id
left outer join priorities on bg_priority = pr_id
left outer join statuses on bg_status = st_id
left outer join users asg on bg_assigned_to_user = asg.us_id
left outer join users ru on bg_reported_user = ru.us_id
left outer join users lu on bg_last_updated_user = lu.us_id
left outer join bug_subscriptions on bs_bug = bg_id and bs_user = 16
left outer join project_user_xref on pj_id = pu_project
and pu_user = 16
where bg_id = 59

/* drop downs */ select pj_id, pj_name
		from projects
		left outer join project_user_xref on pj_id = pu_project
		and pu_user = 16
		where pj_active = 1
		and isnull(pu_permission_level,2) not in (0, 1)
		order by pj_name;
select og_id, og_name from orgs where og_active = 1 order by og_name;
select ct_id, ct_name from categories order by ct_sort_seq, ct_name;
select pr_id, pr_name from priorities order by pr_sort_seq, pr_name;
select st_id, st_name from statuses order by st_sort_seq, st_name;
select udf_id, udf_name from user_defined_attribute order by udf_sort_seq, udf_name;

/* users this project */ select us_id, case when 0 = 1 then us_lastname + ', ' + us_firstname else us_username end us_username
from users
inner join orgs on us_org = og_id
where us_active = 1
and og_can_be_assigned_to = 1
and (2 <> 0 or 1 = og_id or (og_external_user = 0 and 0 = 1))
and us_id not in
	(select pu_user from project_user_xref
		where pu_project = 11
		and pu_permission_level = 0)
order by us_username;
